        function getCookie(cname) {
            var name = cname + "=";
            var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
            for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                var c = ca[i];
                while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1);
                if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
            }
            return "";
        }

        RemoveDiacritics: function (str) {
            if (str==undefined||str.length <= 0) {
                return str;
            }

            if (str.length == 1) {
                var rule = _.find(KafkasApp.Diacritics.DefaultMap, function (obj) { return obj.letters.indexOf(str) !== -1 });
                return (rule != null && rule.base && rule.base.length > 0) ? rule.base : str;
            }

            var result = "";
            for (var i = 0; i < str.length; i++) {
                result += KafkasApp.Diacritics.RemoveDiacritics(str[i]);
            }
            return result;
        }
    },
};
    //console.log(KafkasApp.Diacritics.RemoveDiacritics("ύϋΰΎΫίϊΐΊΪάΆέΈήΉόΌώΏ"));
</script>
